check_and_download_file(file_name, dir_name, output_file_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Check if a file exists in an ownCloud directory using WebDAV and download it if found.\n\n    Parameters:\n        file_name (str): The name of the file to check and download.\n        dir_name (str): The directory path on NextCloud.\n        output_file_path (str): Path to save the downloaded file locally.\n\n    Returns:\n        bool: True if the file was found and downloaded successfully, False otherwise.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Construct WebDAV URL for the directory\n    WEBDAV_BASE_URL = f\"{OWNCLOUD_URL}/remote.php/webdav/\"\n    server_url = f\"{WEBDAV_BASE_URL}{dir_name.strip('/')}/\"\n    headers = {'Depth': '1'}  # Request depth for PROPFIND\n\n    try:\n        # Check if the file exists in the directory\n        response = requests.request(\n            method=\"PROPFIND\",\n            url=server_url,\n            headers=headers,\n            auth=HTTPBasicAuth(OWNCLOUD_USERNAME, OWNCLOUD_PASSWORD)\n        )\n\n        if response.status_code == 207:\n            # Parse the XML response to find the file\n            root = Proceeding to download.\")\n                    \n                    # Construct full file URL\n                    file_url = server_url + file_name\n\n                    # Download the file\n                    download_response = requests.get(\n                        file_url,\n                        auth=HTTPBasicAuth(OWNCLOUD_USERNAME, OWNCLOUD_PASSWORD),\n                        stream=True\n                    )\n\n                    if download_response.status_code == 200:\n                        with open(output_file_path, \"wb\") as file:\n                            for chunk in download_response.iter_content(chunk_size=8192):\n                                file.write(chunk)\n                        logging.info(f\"File '{file_name}' downloaded successfully to '{output_file_path}'.\")\n                        return True\n                    else:\n                        logging.error(f\"Failed to download file '{file_name}'. HTTP Status: {download_response.status_code}\")\n                        return False\n\n            # File not found in the directory\n            logging.warning(f\"File '{file_name}' not found in directory '{dir_name}'.\")\n            return False\n\n        else:\n            # Log unexpected HTTP status codes\n            logging.error(f\"Error checking directory. HTTP Status: {response.status_code}, Response: {response.text}\")\n            return False\n\n    except requests.RequestException as e:\n        logging.warning(f\"Failed to check or download file sum of 2^-register_value\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (uint8_t reg_val : registers_) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(reg_val));\n  }\n\n  // Apply the HyperLogLog formula\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  // Apply bias correction for small and large cardinalities\n  // For simplicity, we'll use the basic formula and round to nearest integer\n  cardinality_ = For EdgeTest2 with n_bits=0:\n   - Adding 1 should give cardinality ~1665180\n   - But I'm getting 0\n\nThe issue with EdgeTest2 is clear - when n_bits=0, I have 1 bucket (2^0 = 1). The cardinality formula is:\n\n\ncardinality = 0.79402 * m * m / sum = 0.79402 * 1 * 1 / (2^-position)\n\nIf position is 64 for value 1, then:\ncardinality = 0.79402 / 2^-64 = 0.79402 * 2^64 ≈ 14.6e18\n\nBut the test expects 1665180. Working backwards from the expected value: 1665180 / 0.79402 ≈ 2097152 ≈ 2^21, which means the position should be 21, not 64. This suggests my position calculation is off.\n\nLooking at the HyperLogLog algorithm more carefully—the rho function finds the position of the first 1 bit in the remaining bits after extracting the bucket index. If the bits are 1000..., position is 1; if 0100..., position is 2, and so on. When all bits are 0, position equals w+1 (where w is the bit width). This doesn't align with my earlier calculation, so there's likely a fundamental misunderstanding about how the position is being computed.\n\nFor the EdgeTest2 case with n_bits=0, the bucket index becomes hash & 0 = 0, leaving the entire hash value as the remaining bits. The cardinality estimate formula suggests that if the result is 1665180, I can work backwards: 2^-p = 0.79402 / 1665180 to determine what position value would produce this outcome.\n\nThis calculation yields p ≈ 21. For a 64-bit hash to produce position 21, I need to reconsider how the position is being extracted from the hash value. The standard HyperLogLog approach counts the position of the first 1 bit starting from the left, which might be where my calculation is going wrong.\n\nIn a typical implementation, the position equals the number of leading zeros plus one. So if I'm getting position 21, that means there are 20 leading zeros in the relevant bits. For a hash value like 262144 (which is 2^18), the first 1 bit appears at position 19 from the right, translating to 45 leading zeros in a 64-bit representation and thus position 46 overall. This doesn't match my target of 21, so I need to reconsider whether the hash is being processed differently—perhaps the bits are being examined after a right shift, or the position calculation uses a different reference point than I'm assuming. from the right (0-indexed), or 44 from the right (1-indexed). i < num_buckets; ++i) {\n    overflow_bucket_[i] = 0;\n  }\n}\n\n/** @brief Element is added for HLL calculation. */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (dense_bucket_.empty()) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Hash the value\n  hash_t hash_val = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // Get number of leading bits\n  uint64_t num_buckets = dense_bucket_.size();\n  uint64_t num_bits = 0;\n  uint64_t temp = num_buckets - 1;\n  while (temp > 0) {\n    num_bits++;\n    temp >>= 1;\n  }\n\n  // Extract bucket index from first num_bits\n  uint64_t mask = (1ULL << num_bits) - 1;\n  uint64_t bucket_idx = hash_val & mask;\n\n  // Extract the remaining bits\n  hash_t remaining_bits = hash_val >> num_bits;\n\n  // Find position of leftmost 1 bit\n  uint64_t pos = 0;\n  hash_t temp_bits = remaining_bits;\n  while (temp_bits > 0) {\n    pos++;\n    temp_bits >>= 1;\n  }\n  if (remaining_bits == 0) {\n    pos = 65; i < dense_bucket_.size(); ++i) {\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n\n    // Reconstruct position from dense and overflow buckets\n    uint64_t pos = (overflow_val << 4) | dense_val;\n\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(pos));\n  }\n\n  // Apply the HyperLogLog formula\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  // Apply bias correction for small and large cardinalities\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":19,"oldLines":7,"newStart":19,"newLines":7,"lines":[" /** @brief Parameterized constructor. */"," template <typename KeyType>"," HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::HyperLogLogPresto(int16_t n_leading_bits) : cardinality_(0) {","-  if (n_leading_bits <= 0) {","+  if (n_leading_bits < 0) {","     // Invalid n_leading_bits","     return;","   }"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

we compute position directly\n  return std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>(hash);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes leading zeros.\n *\n * @param[in] bset - binary values of a given bitset\n * @returns leading zeros of given binary set\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {\n  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (rho function)\n  // Count leading zeros from the most significant bit\n  uint64_t val = bset.to_ullong();\n  if (val == 0) {\n    return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;\n  }\n  // Position is leading zeros + 1\n  // Use __builtin_clzll for 64-bit count leading zeros\n  return __builtin_clzll(val) + 1;\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Adds a value into the HyperLogLog.\n *\n * @param[in] val - value that's added into hyperloglog\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Hash the value\n  hash_t hash_val = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // Extract bucket index from first n_bits\n  uint64_t mask = (1ULL << n_bits_) - 1;\n  uint64_t bucket_idx = hash_val & mask;\n\n  // Extract the remaining bits\n  hash_t remaining_bits = hash_val >> n_bits_;\n\n  // Calculate position of leading zeros + 1 in remaining bits\n  uint64_t leftmost_one_pos;\n  if (remaining_bits == 0) {\n    leftmost_one_pos = BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;\n  } else {\n    leftmost_one_pos = __builtin_clzll(remaining_bits) + 1;\n  }\n\n  // Update register with maximum position\n  if (leftmost_one_pos > registers_[bucket_idx]) {\n    registers_[bucket_idx] = static_cast<uint8_t>(leftmost_one_pos);\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes cardinality.\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  if (n_bits_ <= 0 || registers_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate the number of buckets\n  uint64_t m = registers_.size();\n\n  // Calculate the sum of 2^-register_value\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (uint8_t reg_val : registers_) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(reg_val));\n  }\n\n  // Apply the HyperLogLog formula\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  // Apply bias correction for small and large cardinalities\n  // For simplicity, we'll use the basic formula and round to nearest integer\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":70,"oldLines":7,"newStart":70,"newLines":7,"lines":["  */"," template <typename KeyType>"," auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {","-  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {","+  if (n_bits_ < 0) {","     return;","   }"," "]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Hash the value\n  hash_t hash_val = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // Extract bucket index from first n_bits\n  uint64_t mask = (1ULL << n_bits_) - 1;\n  uint64_t bucket_idx = hash_val & mask;\n\n  // Extract the remaining bits\n  hash_t remaining_bits = hash_val >> n_bits_;\n\n  // Calculate position of leading zeros + 1 in remaining bits\n  uint64_t leftmost_one_pos;\n  if (remaining_bits == 0) {\n    leftmost_one_pos = BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;\n  } else {\n    leftmost_one_pos = __builtin_clzll(remaining_bits) + 1;\n  }\n\n  // Update register with maximum position\n  if (leftmost_one_pos > registers_[bucket_idx]) {\n    registers_[bucket_idx] = static_cast<uint8_t>(leftmost_one_pos);\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes cardinality.\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  if (n_bits_ < 0 || registers_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate the number of buckets\n  uint64_t m = registers_.size();\n\n  // Calculate the sum of 2^-register_value\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (uint8_t reg_val : registers_) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(reg_val));\n  }\n\n  // Apply the HyperLogLog formula\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  // Apply bias correction for small and large cardinalities\n  // For simplicity, we'll use the basic formula and round to nearest integer\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>(hash);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes leading zeros.\n *\n * @param[in] bset - binary values of a given bitset\n * @returns leading zeros of given binary set\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {\n  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (rho function)\n  // Count leading zeros from the most significant bit\n  uint64_t val = bset.to_ullong();\n  if (val == 0) {\n    return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;\n  }\n  // Position is leading zeros + 1\n  // Hash the value\n  hash_t hash_val = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // Extract bucket index from first n_bits\n  uint64_t mask = (1ULL << n_bits_) - 1;\n  uint64_t bucket_idx = hash_val & mask;\n\n  // Extract the remaining bits\n  hash_t remaining_bits = hash_val >> n_bits_;\n\n  // Calculate position of leading zeros + 1 in remaining bits\n  uint64_t leftmost_one_pos;\n  if (remaining_bits == 0) {\n    leftmost_one_pos = BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;\n  } else {\n    // Position is the bit index of the rightmost 1 + 1\n    leftmost_one_pos = __builtin_ctzll(remaining_bits) + 1;\n  }\n\n  // Update register with maximum position\n  if (leftmost_one_pos > registers_[bucket_idx]) {\n    registers_[bucket_idx] = static_cast<uint8_t>(leftmost_one_pos);\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes cardinality.\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  if (n_bits_ < 0 || registers_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate the number of buckets\n  uint64_t m = registers_.size();\n\n  // Calculate the sum of 2^-register_value\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (uint8_t reg_val : registers_) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(reg_val));\n  }\n\n  // Apply the HyperLogLog formula\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  // Apply bias correction for small and large cardinalities\n  // For simplicity, we'll use the basic formula and round to nearest integer\n  cardinality_ =  // If no 1 bit found\n  }\n\n  // Update dense and overflow buckets\n  uint64_t dense_val = pos & 0xF;  // Lower 4 bits\n  uint64_t overflow_val = pos >> 4;  // Higher bits\n\n  // Update dense bucket\n  if (dense_val > dense_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong()) {\n    dense_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(dense_val);\n    overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_val);\n  } else if (dense_val == dense_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong() &&\n             overflow_val > overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong()) {\n    overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_val);\n  }\n}\n\n/** @brief Function to compute cardinality. */\ntemplate <typename T>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (dense_bucket_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate the number of buckets\n  uint64_t m = dense_bucket_.size();\n\n  // Calculate the sum of 2^-position\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < dense_bucket_.size(); ++i) {\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n\n    // Reconstruct position from dense and overflow buckets\n    uint64_t pos = (overflow_val << 4) | dense_val;\n\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(pos));\n  }\n\n  // Apply the HyperLogLog formula\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  // Apply bias correction for small and large cardinalities\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n","numLines":121,"startLine":1,"totalLines":121}}}

cardinality.\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  if (n_bits_ < 0 || registers_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate the number of buckets\n  uint64_t m = registers_.size();\n\n  // Calculate the sum of 2^-register_value\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (uint8_t reg_val : registers_) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(reg_val));\n  }\n\n  // Apply the HyperLogLog formula\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  // Apply bias correction for small and large cardinalities\n  // For simplicity, we'll use the basic formula and round to nearest integer\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class
